< Text>
The way here was extremely adventurous and the road was like a rollercoaster. Arriving at the ranch made it worth it though!

We stayed at the Peacock Tiny House as advertised on Airbnb. It was absolutely incredible. We had our own space to enjoy one another (my husband and I), but also got to say hi to the animals and interact with the very kind  staff. Lina, in the main ranch house, served us an enormously beautiful dinner. When we ordered originally, she mentioned there was no more ribs, but when we arrived, she surprised us with some!!! We were more than full, physically and emotionally. She was so very kind in the entire way she treated us.

At the house itself, there is a roof top deck where you can enjoy the extra warm breeze as you watch the sunset or gaze at the stars. The inside has all the amenities you need and the attention to detail made the entire home super stylish alongside the feel of being welcomed at home. I would most definitely recommend this place.<//Text>

6/1/20
When I reported that the cashier Chantelle or something like that was irritated (written all over her face and she walked away from me without responding. Came back with an irritated look on her face) because I asked her to use hand sanitizer, the store manager Cynthia stated that they get busy there and that the cashier didn't mean it but they do get busy there. I pointed to the line and said, "But that's not the case right now. So there's no excuse because I even offered the employee some of my hand sanitizer. She said nothing and walked off" Either way, NOTHING should be more important than customer safety concerns. Now I feel uncomfortable but I did nothing wrong. I asked Cynthia to check the camera is she thought I was exaggerating, she said she didn't need to but she kept making excuses for the employee. Cynthia needs to remember she is not there to take business away from the company (Just the opposite) by dismissing customer concerns, it's bad for business.

Owner or district manager please address this issue to save lives. It makes you very uncomfortable when the cashier gets huffy about a reasonable request. Dollar Tree website states gloves and masks provided to employees. FYI fact! This cashier employee did not have on gloves. Just her bare hands which recently touch dollar bills and coins. This is what sparked my concerns initially.

6/2/20
Today, I called back after thinking about it, after reading Dollar Tree code of ethics, to explain to Cynthia that I don't feel her answer was acceptable. Did not meet company standards for customer care. Nothing should come before customer safety, staff should always be happy to oblige when asked to help ensure customer safety. No excuses necessary. Customers should feel safe. Covid 19 is a person to person contact pandemic. I wasn't making an unreasonable request.

Cynthia was dismissive today, only saying uh huh. Coincidentally the phone magically hug up and the line is now busy constantly.

Other employees know that I am a regular customer, friendly, easy going. But I have a right to protect my health. Especially because I am a nurse with asthma. Which I told Cynthia.

The other Dollar Tree on Bristol/Alton NEVER gives excuses, always understands when I asked an employee to use hand sanitizer. Chris and staff are examples for all stores to follow They oblige in a friendly and caring manner which shows they actually care about the customer. But Dollar Tree locations should function the same. Never question a consumer's right to remain safe.

The previous manager at FV location was excellent and handled customer concerns extremely well. Cynthia isn't qualified to deal with customers safety concerns if she has to take the phone off the hook, and tells a customer basically the line is more important than their safety. Pretty sure Dollar Tree risk management dept and Gary Philbin would take issue with her answer.</Text>

< Text>
Cash only. Pineapple buns are a Hong Kong food, pineapple referring to the design of the topping on the bun. So don't come expecting pineapple flavored buns. However, these buns are DELICIOUS. They have every option under the sun (bbq pork, pizza, plain, with butter) and they are all sweet, delicious and cheap. The butter buns come with A SLAB of butter. Yum!< /Text>

<Review>The first time I've tasted a pineapple bun was at this place. I've never heard of it before so I really thought it had pineapples in it. So, during my first trip, I bought one pineapple bun. When I got home, I bit into it and immediately had to tell someone how good it was!

Since I live quite far from here, I've been searching everywhere for pineapple buns and have been disappointed... The reason was because I realized pineapple bun was just a sweet bread. What I had gotten at Pineapple King Bakery was a pineapple bun with custard. I highly highly recommend it! Once I realized my mistake, I made it a quest to go there and buy as many as I can because I couldn't find it anywhere else. So this was my second trip; I bought 2 pineapple buns with custard, a pineapple bun with red bean and one with pineapple.
The one with custard is a very popular item and sells pretty quick.

So, if you don't know what a pineapple bun is, it's usually sweet bun in which the top is scored like a pineapple. The top of it looks like the skin of a pineapple.

The workers are super nice and efficient.
Since this is a small store, there are no restrooms, but there is one really close by at the Golden Gate Park in case you need one.

Overall, I would definitely keep coming back for these buns and the egg tarts :D< /Review>< Pictures>

<text>** During Quarantine Review **

I was casually browsing my yelp app when I saw this cute bakery just a block away. With the high ratings and limited open food options available we decided to check it out. On our visit there was a small line that formed just outside the store, but it moved very quickly.

The menu was pretty confusing and lengthy. I really had no idea what to order, but the customer in front of me said that the butter pineapple bun was the most popular and recommended the deluxe box, so we went ahead and ordered that.

My friend and I split everything and here's our verdict

I really like the pineapple bun! It has a nice sweet crusty flavor; however, my some fillings were better than others. The butter (orginal) was very lackluster to me. It tasted like the individual butter packs that you get at the diner to slather in the dinner rolls. It didn't add anything in my opinion. The matcha and custard fillings on the other-hand had that perfect amount of sweetness. The mango was way too overpowering.

Now that I know what pineapple buns taste like I think on my next visit I'll know what to order. I'd love to try the ube and I'm super curious about trying some of their savory options like spam and bbq pork. Stick to the asian flavors and you won't be disappointed!<//text><user_id>100420235279118081561</user_id><pictures>None<//pictures>< Rating>

< text>
Hidden gem in the area they have amazing pineapple cream buns I particularly enjoyed the matcha cream. It's only $1.60 for two buns super great value! They have different breads as well from sweet to savory!  The pork buns are worth checking out as well!

They only take cash so make sure you have some before you get there.

They also do phone orders if you're ordering large orders for parties. Service is pretty quick if it's an empty shop but if there's a line prepared to wait about 5-10 minutes extra, but overall it's a pretty quick in and out trip.

There's no tables here to enjoy your treats unfortunately. There is also no bathroom here either .</text>

< Review>
They serve the best pineapple bun in the world. I am in my 40s and grew up in Hong Kong. A good pineapple bun was what my childhood is all about. I have to say, it is very difficult to find a good pineapple bun in HK nowadays. Thanks God for Pineapple King. Their buns (yes, all of the other varieties as well) are just like the way they used to make it. For the best possible buns, come at 7:30 am when all the buns are rolling off the oven. Couple with their equally good HK milk tea.... I especially recommend all of their pineapple buns will filling. They are all amazing!< /Review>

<rating>5</rating><name>Emily Yush Yuen</name>< Review>
As a Hong Kong local, I maintain that this Hong Kong style bakery bakes bread that beats most Hong Kong bakeries. They reheat bread on request. Their pineapple bun is indeed the best, with a crispy topping atop a soft bun. All their breads are however, superb. Their pastries are also excellent - the taro pastry has just the right amount of sweetness to bring out the taro flavour. And to top this all off is their Hong Kong milk tea, especially when made by Ivy, beats ALL Hong Kong milk tea places. The tea is stronger than expresso coffee, smooth and is perfectly sweet at regular sweetness. I'd go every day if cholesterol wasn't a concern.< /Review>

< Text>
Triangle Tattoo & Museum in Fort Bragg California is one amazing place to experience!

Mr G. was kind enough to attend a Career Day Zoom presentation as guest speaker for one of our high school classes. He was scheduled for a half hour time slot but was asked to stay  for an hour!

His presentation covered the History of where, why, who, and how body painting got started. And how it progressed to modern day. He had a terrific slide show depicted the many cultures across the world use of it.

He covered how women became part of it and why. How the depression and wars played a part in it and so much more. Mr. G shared his personal experiences in tattooing.

He is an amazing tattoo artist that is highly knowledgeable, skilled, amiable, imagineable,
Creative, and respectful.

The Museum part is equally as amazing g as it has historic tools and images to enjoy and be intrigued by. It is a must see!

He is coming back for an encore!!!<//Text>

< Review>
Firstly, I‚Äôd like to mention that I‚Äôve only ever given 2 reviews before this. I‚Äôm not often inspired or motivated to give a review, so this should already tell you something.

Madame Chinchilla and Mr. G are by far the greatest people you will ever encounter. They‚Äôre chock-full of stories from their wild days, which always make for great conversation throughout your piece, and are extremely welcoming and friendly. Madame Chinchilla was keen on accommodating me (a last minute arrival) despite busy schedules and a nearing closing time. Mr. G was able to take me on last minute without any fuss. A true gentleman. The piece itself was quite small (I was only in town for that night, so a quickie was necessary‚Äìplus, they were closing soon), and a Sailor Jerry tattoo, but Mr. G treated it as if it meant more to me (it does now). Spectacular work, great shading, professionalism. I‚Äôll update with a photo at a later time when it‚Äôs all healed up. What was initially supposed to be a ‚Äújust because‚Äù tattoo, became even more through the experience, detail and love put into it.

With regard to the museum, it is completely riddled with varying styles of tattoos, their histories, equipments used over the years and photos of Madame Chinchilla and Mr. G throughout their years together (super cute couple btw). There are also a number of books with interesting facts about tattoo culture and history as well as stories of interesting people and their equally interesting body art.

We‚Äôll definitely be coming back! Madame Chinchilla says it so. Thank you both for the wonderfully memorable experience!< /Review>

<gmapID>0x80803548e7dc01ed:0x1e6bfbb945600c8f</gmapID><user_name>Zoey K<//user_name>< text>
I love how they have transformed this tiny tattoo shop into a sort of museum. It definitely is VERY small, so if you are claustrophobic or get dizzy easily, I don't recommend staying for too long. The amount of tattoo history they have covering their walls is fascinating. As we are walking through, we keep seeing photos of this "Madame Chinchilla and Mr. G" and think, "oh those must be some cool famous tattoo people." Suddenly a older woman comes out and starts asking us about the museum and tells us stories about tattooing and come to find out it is Madame Chinchilla herself! She is very sweet and so knowledgeable. I wish I had the time to get tattooed there! Next time I'm in Mendocino I'll have to schedule an appointment!< /text>

<rating>3< /rating>< Review>
I am editing this review and downgrade it to 3 stars. They took out the best thing on the menu, grilled Liemsilog. Why? Why? Why?

One of the rare places that open late in downtown Hayward, even though it's only the weekend. The seating is quite small, so if you are hungry at 1AM Saturday morning prepare to do take out instead.

Their service is quick, food is cheap and tasty, even though it can be done with less meat and a little more veggie for my taste. The eating area is fairly clean even though the fryer is so close so prepare to have your clothes smell like grease after eating. Parking in downtown Hayward is fairly easy to find.

For 6.99, I rate it as one of the best value meal you can get in this area.< /Review>

<review>Tapsilog Express, you will always have a special place in my heart, and I'm not just talking about the grease left behind by all your food.

This is the comfort food that leaves your belly full but your wallet happy whether it is 1am on a Saturday night or Sunday when you're hungover the next day.  All the dishes come with your choice form of protein, garlic rice, egg, and a lonely slice of tomato.  The garlic rice has been better since the place opened but no silog meal would be complete without it.  Service is usually quick but they have their occasional rushes where you question whether you could have made it yourself faster.  The halo-halo here is legit and does satisfy your sweet tooth. If you find that you are extra hungry, add an extra egg... or heck, order another dish.</review>< GmapID>

< Review>
Habit ran a great promotion in March where they offered a free burger if you registered with their website.

I took them up on the offer since they have a location about a mile and a half from my house.

In all honesty, I was pretty blown away by the quality of the food. They make a delicious burger and I've since been back to try their strawberry & grilled chicken salad which was also excellent. I hope they'll consider making it a permanent addition to their menu.

These days, there are a lot of places you can go to get a burger, but I'll vouch for Habit being one of the better options.</Review>
